    command_run(command: Command) {
      for (const seq of command.sequence ?? []) {
        this.command_run(seq)

        if (this.paused) {
          this.paused = false
          throw new Error('paused')

        }
      }

      if (command.gather) {
        $mol_wire_race(...command.gather.map(cmd => () => this.command_run(cmd)))
      }
      if (command.message) this.message(command.message)
      if (command.pause) this.pause(command.pause)

      if (command.stop) this.stop()
      if (command.music) this.background_music_uri(command.music.src)

  function data_traverse(val: $mol_data_value) {
    if (val === $mol_data_string) return 'string'
    if (val === $mol_data_number) return 'number'
    if (val === $mol_data_boolean) return 'boolean'
    if (val?.config?.pattern) return val.config.pattern.source
    if (val?.config?.nullable) return `${data_traverse(val?.config?.nullable)} | null`
    if (val?.config?.array) return `${data_traverse(val.config?.array)}[]`
    if (val?.config?.dict) return `Record<string, ${data_traverse(val.config.dict)}>`
    if (val?.config?.record) {
      let object_string = '{\n'
      for (const key of Object.keys(val.config.record)) {
        const sub = val.config.record[key]
        object_string += `  ${key}${sub.config?.optional ? '?' : ''}: ${data_traverse(sub)},\n`
      }
      object_string += '}'
      return object_string
    }
  }

Sergey Yuferev 
  const cache = new WeakMap<Object, Error>()

  export function $mol_error_improve(e: unknown, cause: Object) {
    const err = e instanceof Error ? e : new Error(String(e), { cause: e })

    let improved = cache.get(err)
    if (! improved) {
      improved = new $mol_error_mix(err.message, err, new Error('improved', { cause }))
      cache.set(err, improved)
    }

    return improved
  }
